####################
# COUNTRIES / PAYS #
####################

###Ex.: [le] Pont / [la] Sogdiane / [l']Empire séleucide / [les] Diablintes / [Ø]Carthage
get_LeLaLNP = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				#sg_art_masc_cons_lg_01 = yes
				sg_art_masc_cons_sh_02 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_la
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06_REVOLT = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_sh_07 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_art_masc_vow_lg1_03 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_lg2_04 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_sh_05 = yes
				sg_art_fem_vow_sh_09 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_les
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				pl_masc_coll_18 = yes
				pl_fem_geo_21 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_noart_masc_cons_sh_11 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_vow_sh_13 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_cons_sh_15 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_vow_sh_17 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}


###Ex.: qui [l']entoure (= Rome) / qui [les] entourent (= les Diablintes)
get_LLesNP = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				#sg_art_masc_cons_lg_01 = yes
				sg_art_masc_cons_sh_02 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_lg1_03 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_lg2_04 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_sh_05 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06_REVOLT = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_sh_07 = yes
				sg_art_fem_vow_sh_09 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_cons_sh_11 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_vow_sh_13 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_cons_sh_15 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_vow_sh_17 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_les
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				pl_masc_coll_18 = yes
				pl_fem_geo_21 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

###Ex.: [au] Pont / [dans le] Royaume du Bosphore / [en] Sogdiane / [dans la] Ligue des Nésiotes / [dans l']Empire séleucide / [à] Carthage / [chez les] Diablintes / [dans les] Gymnésies
get_AuEnANP = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_au
		trigger = {
			sg_art_masc_cons_sh_02 = yes
		}
	}
#	text = {
#		localization_key = frloc_dansle
#		trigger = {
#			sg_art_masc_cons_lg_01 = yes
#		}
#	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_en
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_art_masc_vow_lg2_04 = yes
				sg_art_masc_vow_sh_05 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_sh_07 = yes
				sg_art_fem_vow_sh_09 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_dansla
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06_REVOLT = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_dansl
		trigger = {
			sg_art_masc_vow_lg1_03 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_a02
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_noart_masc_cons_sh_11 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_vow_sh_13 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_cons_sh_15 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_vow_sh_17 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_chezles
		trigger = {
			pl_masc_coll_18 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_dansles
		trigger = {
			pl_fem_geo_21 = yes
		}
	}
}


###Ex.: [notre] vassale Rome / [nos] vassaux les Diablintes

				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06_REVOLT = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_sh_07 = yes
				sg_art_fem_vow_sh_09 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_cons_sh_11 = yes
				sg_noart_masc_vow_sh_13 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_cons_sh_15 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_vow_sh_17 = yes
			}
		}

			OR = {
				pl_masc_coll_18 = yes
				pl_fem_geo_21 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

###Ex.: [s'il] est attaqué (= le Pont) / [si elle] est attaquée (= la Sogdiane) / [s'ils] sont attaqués (= les Diablintes) / [si elles] sont attaquées (= les Gymnésies)

	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_sil

			OR = {

			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_sielle
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06 = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_lg_06_REVOLT = yes
				sg_art_fem_cons_sh_07 = yes
				sg_art_fem_vow_sh_09 = yes
				sg_noart_fem_cons_sh_15 = yes

###Ex.: [le] Gandhara / [l']Himalaya / [la] Mésopotamie / [l']Assyrie / [Ø]Pount
get_LeLaLRegion = {
	type = province
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			region_sg_art_masc_cons_01 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_la
		trigger = {
			region_sg_art_fem_cons_03 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				region_sg_art_masc_vow_02 = yes
				region_sg_art_fem_vow_04 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			region_sg_no_art_masc_cons_05 = yes
		}
	}
}
###Ex.: [le] Norique / [l']Aurès / [la] Babylonie / [l']Assyrie / [Ø]Pount / [Ø]Chypre / [Ø]Ultima Thulé / [les] Monts Porphyrites / [les] Alpes grées
get_LeLaLProvince = {
	type = province
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			province_sg_art_masc_cons_01 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_la
		trigger = {
			province_sg_art_fem_cons_03 = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				province_sg_art_masc_vow_02 = yes
				province_sg_art_fem_vow_04 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				province_sg_no_art_masc_cons_05 = yes
				province_sg_no_art_fem_cons_07 = yes
				province_sg_no_art_fem_vow_08 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_les
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				province_pl_art_masc_cons_09 = yes
				province_pl_art_masc_vow_10 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

###Ex.: [le] juge / [l']ancien // [la] juge / [l']ancienne
get_LeLaLOffice = {
	type = character
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				### Tribes / Tribus
				AND = { has_office = office_arbitrator is_female = no } # Juge (+ _hellenic Kritês)
				AND = { has_office = office_warchief is_female = no } # Chef de guerre (+ _hellenic Polémarque)
				AND = { has_office = office_bodyguard is_female = no } # Garde du corps (+ _hellenic Sômatophylaque)
				AND = { has_office = office_high_priest is_female = no } # Grand prêtre (+ _hellenic Hiérophante)
				AND = { has_office = office_wise_person is_female = no } # Sage (+ _hellenic Sophos)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_magistrate is_female = no # Magistrat
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Archonte)
				}
				### Republics / Républiques
				AND = { has_office = office_censor is_female = no } # Censeur (+ _indian _aryan _tibetan Mantri + _persia Databdara + _hellenic Thesmothète + _west_levantine Shephat)
				AND = { has_office = office_praetor is_female = no } # Magistrat (+ _latin Préteur + _indian _aryan + _tibetan Pradeshtri + _persia Spahbed + _hellenic Prytane)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_soldiers is_female = no # Tribun des soldats (+ _latin Tribun des soldats + _indian _aryan _tibetan Senapati + _hellenic Stratège + _west_levantine Mefahked)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = persia } } # (Argbadh)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_treasury is_female = no # Tribun du trésor (+ _latin Préfet militaire + _indian _aryan _tibetan Karanika + _persia Salar)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Aréopage)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_augur is_female = no # (Augure)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Mogh
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Dadouque
					}
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_pontifex is_female = no } # Grand prêtre (+ _latin Grand pontife + _indian _aryan _tibetan Purohita + _persia Mobadan mobad + _hellenic Hiérophante + _west_levantine Kahen)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_plebeian_aedile is_female = no # Tribun du peuple (+ _latin Tribun de la plèbe + _indian _aryan _tibetan Karmika)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # (Artabid)
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Agoranome)
					}
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_republic_physician is_female = no } # Médecin (+ _latin Vulnéraire + _indian _aryan _tibetan Vaidya + _west_levantine Rophet)
				### Monarchies / Monarchies ###
				AND = {
					has_office = office_foreign_minister is_female = no # Chancelier (+ _latin Chancelier + _aryan _indian _tibetan Prasastr + _persia Databdara)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Épiproxène)
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # (Amerkhatnébout)
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_royal_tutor is_female = no # Tuteur royal (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Sunyapala + _hellenic Tropheus + _north_african Sakhadshout)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = persia } } # (Arzbad-e-Aspwaragan)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_marshal is_female = no # Maréchal (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Senapati + _west_levantine Mefahked + _north_african Hatjya)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # (Argbadh)
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Épistratège)
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_master_of_the_guard is_female = no # Maître de la Garde (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Dauvarika + _persia Spahbed + _west_levantine Shohmer)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Archisomatophylaque)
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # (Amérawahyet)
					}
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_high_priest_monarchy is_female = no } # Grand prêtre (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Purohita + _persia Mobadan mobad + _hellenic Hiérophante + _west_levantine Kahen + _north_african Hruhbdjet)
				AND = { has_office = office_philosopher is_female = no } # Philosophe de la cour (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Mantri + _persia Mogh + _hellenic Philosophe + _north_african Xrahub)
				AND = {

						employer = { country_culture_group = indian } # Samnidhatr

					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Archiatre)
				}

						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Agoranome // Agoranome
					}
				}
				### Monarchies / Monarchies ###
				AND = {
					has_office = office_foreign_minister # (Chancelier) // (Chancelière)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Épiproxène // Épiproxène
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # Amerkhatnébout // Amerkhatnébout
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_royal_tutor # (Tuteur royal) // (Tutrice royale)
					employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Arzbad-e-Aspwaragan // Arzbad-e-Aspwaragan)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_marshal # (Maréchal) // (Maréchale)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Argbadh // Argbadh 
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Épistratège // Épistratège
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_master_of_the_guard # (Maître de la Garde) // (Maîtresse de la Garde)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Archisomatophylaque
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # Amérawahyet
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_steward # Intendant // Intendante (+ _persia Artabid + _hellenic Archigrammate + _north_african Iry-pat)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = aryan } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = indian } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = tibetan } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = west_levantine } # (Shephat)
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_physician # (Médecin) // (Médecienne)
					employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Archiatre // Archiatre
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###Ex.: [au] juge / [à l']ancien // [à la] juge / [à l']ancienne
get_AuAlaAlOffice = {
	type = character
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_au
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				### Tribes / Tribus
				AND = { has_office = office_arbitrator is_female = no } # Juge (+ _hellenic Kritês)
				AND = { has_office = office_warchief is_female = no } # Chef de guerre (+ _hellenic Polémarque)
				AND = { has_office = office_bodyguard is_female = no } # Garde du corps (+ _hellenic Sômatophylaque)
				AND = { has_office = office_high_priest is_female = no } # Grand prêtre (+ _hellenic Hiérophante)
				AND = { has_office = office_wise_person is_female = no } # Sage (+ _hellenic Sophos)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_magistrate is_female = no # Magistrat
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Archonte)
				}
				### Republics / Républiques
				AND = { has_office = office_censor is_female = no } # Censeur (+ _indian _aryan _tibetan Mantri + _persia Databdara + _hellenic Thesmothète + _west_levantine Shephat)
				AND = { has_office = office_praetor is_female = no } # Magistrat (+ _latin Préteur + _indian _aryan + _tibetan Pradeshtri + _persia Spahbed + _hellenic Prytane)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_soldiers is_female = no # Tribun des soldats (+ _latin Tribun des soldats + _indian _aryan _tibetan Senapati + _hellenic Stratège + _west_levantine Mefahked)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = persia } } # (Argbadh)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_treasury is_female = no # Tribun du trésor (+ _latin Préfet militaire + _indian _aryan _tibetan Karanika + _persia Salar)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Aréopage)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_augur is_female = no # (Augure)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Mogh
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Dadouque
					}
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_pontifex is_female = no } # Grand prêtre (+ _latin Grand pontife + _indian _aryan _tibetan Purohita + _persia Mobadan mobad + _hellenic Hiérophante + _west_levantine Kahen)
				AND = {

				### Monarchies / Monarchies ###
				AND = {
					has_office = office_foreign_minister is_female = no # Chancelier (+ _latin Chancelier + _aryan _indian _tibetan Prasastr + _persia Databdara)
					NOR = {

						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Archisomatophylaque)
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # (Amérawahyet)
					}
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_high_priest_monarchy is_female = yes } # Grande prêtresse (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Purohita + _persia Mobadan mobad + _hellenic Hiérophante + _west_levantine Kahen + _north_african Hruhbdjet)
				AND = { has_office = office_philosopher is_female = yes } # Philosophe de la cour (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Mantri + _persia Mogh + _hellenic Philosophe + _north_african Xrahub)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_steward is_female = yes # (Intendante)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = aryan } # Samnidhatr
						employer = { country_culture_group = indian } # Samnidhatr
						employer = { country_culture_group = tibetan } # Samnidhatr
						employer = { country_culture_group = west_levantine } # Shephat
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_physician is_female = yes # Médecienne (+ _aryan _indian _tibetan Vaidya + _west_levantine Rophet + _north_african Sunu)
					NOT = { employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } } # (Archiatre)
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				### Tribes / Tribus ###
				AND = { has_office = office_elder } # Ancien (+ _hellenic = Abbas) // Ancienne (+ _hellenic Arkhaïa)
				AND = {
					has_office = office_magistrate # (Magistrat) // (Magistrate)
					employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Archonte // Archonte
				}
				AND = { has_office = office_apothecary } # Apothicaire (+ _hellenic Archiatre) // Apothicaire (+ _hellenic Archiatre)
				### Republics / Républiques ###
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_soldiers # (Tribun des soldats) // (Tribun des soldats)
					employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Argbadh // Argbadh
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_tribune_of_the_treasury # (Tribun du trésor) // (Tribun du trésor)
					employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Aréopage // Aréopage
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_augur # Augure // Augure
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # (Mogh) // (Mogh) 
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # (Dadouque) // (Dadouque)
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_plebeian_aedile # (Tribun du peuple)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Artabid // Artabid
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Agoranome // Agoranome
					}
				}
				### Monarchies / Monarchies ###
				AND = {
					has_office = office_foreign_minister # (Chancelier) // (Chancelière)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Épiproxène // Épiproxène
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # Amerkhatnébout // Amerkhatnébout
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_royal_tutor # (Tuteur royal) // (Tutrice royale)
					employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Arzbad-e-Aspwaragan // Arzbad-e-Aspwaragan)
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_marshal # (Maréchal) // (Maréchale)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = persia } # Argbadh // Argbadh 
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Épistratège // Épistratège
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_master_of_the_guard # (Maître de la Garde) // (Maîtresse de la Garde)
					OR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Archisomatophylaque
						employer = { country_culture_group = north_african } # Amérawahyet
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_steward # Intendant // Intendante (+ _persia Artabid + _hellenic Archigrammate + _north_african Iry-pat)
					NOR = {
						employer = { country_culture_group = aryan } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = indian } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = tibetan } # (Samnidhatr)
						employer = { country_culture_group = west_levantine } # (Shephat)
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_office = office_physician # (Médecin) // (Médecienne)
					employer = { country_culture_group = hellenic } # Archiatre // Archiatre
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	text = {
		localization_key = jealous
		trigger = {
#			has_trait = jealous
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = jealous_female
		trigger = {
#			has_trait = jealous
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frail
		trigger = {
#			has_trait = frail
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		}
	}

		trigger = {
			party = mercantile_party
		}
	}
	text = {

		}

		}
	}

get_LeLaLRelN = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = egyptian_pantheon
				religion = carthaginian_pantheon
				religion = shamanism
				religion = druidism
				religion = judaism
				religion = zoroaster
				religion = matrist_religion
				religion = berber_religion
				religion = germanic_religion
				religion = eastern_animism
				religion = buddhism
				religion = bon_religion
				religion = anatolian_religion
				religion = armenian_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = jainism
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_l
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = roman_pantheon
				religion = animism
				religion = arabian_pantheon
				religion = hindu
				religion = indo_iranian_religion
				religion = caucasian_religion
			}
		}
	}
}

				religion = judaism
				religion = zoroaster
				religion = matrist_religion
				religion = berber_religion
				religion = germanic_religion
				religion = eastern_animism
				religion = buddhism
				religion = bon_religion
				religion = anatolian_religion
				religion = armenian_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = jainism
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_del
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = roman_pantheon
				religion = animism
				religion = arabian_pantheon
				religion = hindu
				religion = indo_iranian_religion
				religion = caucasian_religion
			}
		}
	}
}

###Ex.: Untel s'est converti(e) [au] druidisme / [à l']hellénisme
get_AuAlaAlRelNPers = {
	type = character
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_au
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_religion = egyptian_pantheon
				has_religion = carthaginian_pantheon
				has_religion = shamanism
				has_religion = druidism
				has_religion = judaism
				has_religion = zoroaster
				has_religion = matrist_religion
				has_religion = berber_religion
				has_religion = germanic_religion
				has_religion = eastern_animism
				has_religion = buddhism
				has_religion = bon_religion
				has_religion = anatolian_religion
				has_religion = mesopotamian_religion
				has_religion = jainism
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_al
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_religion = roman_pantheon
				has_religion = animism
				has_religion = arabian_pantheon
				has_religion = hindu
				has_religion = indo_iranian_religion
				has_religion = armenian_religion
				has_religion = caucasian_religion
			}
		}
	}
}

### Court Type / Type de cour ###
#Ex.: [la] cour / [le] Sénat / [le] Conseil des clans
get_LeLaL_court_type = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_republic = yes
				is_tribal = yes
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_la
		trigger = {
				is_monarchy = yes
		}
	}
}

	type = country

	text = {
		localization_key = got_tribal_council_type_plural
		trigger = {
			is_tribal = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_republic_council_type_plural
		trigger = {
			is_republic = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_monarchy_council_type_plural
		trigger = {
			is_monarchy = yes
		}
	}
}

	text = {
		localization_key = get_god_gods_LeLaLes
		trigger = {
			OR = {

				religion = zoroaster
			}
		}

		}
	}

		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
}

### Rival Description / Description du rival ###
#Ex. [l'odieux] NH / [l'odieuse] NF
get_LeLa_rival_adjective = {
	type = character
	random_valid = yes
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_1
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_1_female
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_2
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_2_female
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_3
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = rival_adjective_3_female
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}

### Age Description / Description selon l'âge ###
#Ex. un [jeune homme] / une [jeune femme]
get_age_description_FR = {
	type = character
	text = {
		localization_key = got_child
		trigger = {
			is_adult = no
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_child_female
		trigger = {
			is_adult = no
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_youth
		trigger = {
			is_adult = yes
			age < 22
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_youth_female
		trigger = {
			is_adult = yes
			age < 22
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_average_age
		trigger = {
			age >= 22
			age < 35
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_average_age_female
		trigger = {
			age >= 22
			age < 35
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_older_person
		trigger = {
			age >= 35
			age < 50
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_older_person_female
		trigger = {
			age >= 35
			age < 50
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_ancient_person
		trigger = {
			age >= 50
			age < 70
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {

		trigger = {
			age >= 50
			age < 70

		}
	}
	text = {

		trigger = {
			age >= 70
			age < 100
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = got_methuselah_female
		trigger = {
			age >= 70
			age < 100
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {

			age >= 100

		}

#Ex. [ø] Marduk / [le] dieu de la guerre // [ø] Ishtar / [la] déesse de l'amour
# Male Gods (Medicine) / Dieux de la médecine
get_LeLa_medicine_god_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Esculape (Roman get_aesculapius)
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Vetis (Etruscan get_vetis)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Asclépios (Hellenic get_asclepius)
				religion = carthaginian_pantheon # Eshmoun (Canaanite get_eshmun)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Imhotep (Kemetic get_imhotep)
				religion = druidism # Belenos (Chaldean get_belenos)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Nusku (Chaldean get_nusku)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_le
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "dieu de la médecine" (get_medicine_god_default)
		}
	}
}
# Male Gods (War) / Dieux de la guerre

				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Anhur (Kemetic get_anhur)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Ninurta (Chaldean get_ninurta)
				religion = druidism # Toutatis (Druidic get_toutatis)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)

get_LeLa_hero_god_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Hercule (Roman get_hercules)
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Hercle (Etruscan get_hercle)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Héraclès (Hellenic get_heracles)
				religion = carthaginian_pantheon # Melqart (Canaanite get_melqart)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Heryshef (Kemetic get_heryshaf)
				religion = druidism # Ogmios (Druidic get_ogmios)
				religion = indo_iranian_religion # Targitaos (Heptadic get_targitaos)

# Female Goddesses (Harvest) / Déesses de la moisson
get_LeLa_harvest_goddess_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_empty
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Cérès (Roman get_ceres)
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Cel (Etruscan get_cels)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Déméter (Hellenic get_demeter)
				AND = { country_culture_group = latin religion = anatolian_religion } # Magna Mater (Latin get_magna_mater)
				religion = anatolian_religion # Cybèle (Cybelene get_cybele)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Isis (Kemetic get_isis)
				AND = { country_culture = aquitani religion = druidism } # Mari (Aquitani get_mari)
				religion = armenian_religion # Huba (Khaldic get_huba)
				religion = caucasian_religion # Anahit (Armazic get_anahit)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Shâla (Chaldean get_shala)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = aquitani } religion = druidism } # Rosmerta (Druidic get_rosmerta)
				religion = germanic_religion # Nerthuz (Tuistic get_nerthus)
				religion = matrist_religion # Saulia (Matrist get_saulia)
				religion = berber_religion # Isis (Megalithic get_isis)
				religion = shamanism # Sémélé (Zalmoxian get_semele)
				religion = indo_iranian_religion # Argimpasa (Heptadic get_argimpasa)
				religion = arabian_pantheon # ar-Rabba (Arabic get_orotalt)
				religion = zoroaster # Spenta Armaiti (Zoroaster get_tishtrya)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Jewish get_jewish_god)
				religion = hindu # Parvati (Hindu get_parvati)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = jainism # Mahavira (Jain get_mahavir)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_les
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = animism # (les) Duillae (Iberic get_the_duillae)
				OR = { religion = eastern_animism religion = bon_religion } # (les) ancêtres (Ritualistic/Bon get_the_ancestors)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_la
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la moisson" (get_harvest_goddess_default)
		}
	}
}

				religion = druidism # Belenos (Chaldean get_belenos)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Nusku (Chaldean get_nusku)

				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Dionysos (Hellenic get_dionysus)
				religion = anatolian_religion # Sabazios (Cybelene get_sabazios)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Osiris (Kemetic get_osiris)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_au
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "dieu du vin" (get_wine_god_default)
		}
	}
}

# Female Goddesses (Harvest) / Déesses de la moisson
get_AAuAla_harvest_goddess_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_a02
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Cérès (Roman get_ceres)
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Cel (Etruscan get_cels)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Déméter (Hellenic get_demeter)
				AND = { country_culture_group = latin religion = anatolian_religion } # Magna Mater (Latin get_magna_mater)
				religion = anatolian_religion # Cybèle (Cybelene get_cybele)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Isis (Kemetic get_isis)
				AND = { country_culture = aquitani religion = druidism } # Mari (Aquitani get_mari)
				religion = armenian_religion # Huba (Khaldic get_huba)
				religion = caucasian_religion # Anahit (Armazic get_anahit)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Shâla (Chaldean get_shala)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = aquitani } religion = druidism } # Rosmerta (Druidic get_rosmerta)
				religion = germanic_religion # Nerthuz (Tuistic get_nerthus)
				religion = matrist_religion # Saulia (Matrist get_saulia)
				religion = berber_religion # Isis (Megalithic get_isis)
				religion = shamanism # Sémélé (Zalmoxian get_semele)
				religion = indo_iranian_religion # Argimpasa (Heptadic get_argimpasa)
				religion = arabian_pantheon # ar-Rabba (Arabic get_orotalt)
				religion = zoroaster # Spenta Armaiti (Zoroaster get_tishtrya)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Jewish get_jewish_god)
				religion = hindu # Parvati (Hindu get_parvati)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = jainism # Mahavira (Jain get_mahavir)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_aux
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = animism # (les) Duillae (Iberic get_the_duillae)
				OR = { religion = eastern_animism religion = bon_religion } # (les) ancêtres (Ritualistic/Bon get_the_ancestors)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_ala
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la moisson" (get_harvest_goddess_default)
		}
	}
}

# Male Gods (Medicine) / Dieux de la médecine
get_DeDuDela_medicine_god_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_de
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Vetis (Etruscan get_vetis)
				religion = druidism # Belenos (Chaldean get_belenos)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Nusku (Chaldean get_nusku)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Esculape (Roman get_aesculapius)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Asclépios (Hellenic get_asclepius)
				religion = carthaginian_pantheon # Eshmoun (Canaanite get_eshmun)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Imhotep (Kemetic get_imhotep)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_du
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "dieu de la médecine" (get_medicine_god_default)
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

# Female Goddesses (Harvest) / Déesses de la moisson
get_DeDuDela_harvest_goddess_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_de
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Cérès (Roman get_ceres)
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Cel (Etruscan get_cels)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Déméter (Hellenic get_demeter)
				AND = { country_culture_group = latin religion = anatolian_religion } # Magna Mater (Latin get_magna_mater)
				religion = anatolian_religion # Cybèle (Cybelene get_cybele)
				AND = { country_culture = aquitani religion = druidism } # Mari (Aquitani get_mari)
				religion = armenian_religion # Huba (Khaldic get_huba)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Shâla (Chaldean get_shala)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = aquitani } religion = druidism } # Rosmerta (Druidic get_rosmerta)
				religion = germanic_religion # Nerthuz (Tuistic get_nerthus)
				religion = matrist_religion # Saulia (Matrist get_saulia)
				religion = shamanism # Sémélé (Zalmoxian get_semele)
				religion = zoroaster # Spenta Armaiti (Zoroaster get_tishtrya)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Jewish get_jewish_god)
				religion = hindu # Parvati (Hindu get_parvati)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = jainism # Mahavira (Jain get_mahavir)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Isis (Kemetic get_isis)
				religion = caucasian_religion # Anahit (Armazic get_anahit)
				religion = berber_religion # Isis (Megalithic get_isis)
				religion = indo_iranian_religion # Argimpasa (Heptadic get_argimpasa)
				religion = arabian_pantheon # ar-Rabba (Arabic get_orotalt)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_des
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = animism # (les) Duillae (Iberic get_the_duillae)
				OR = { religion = eastern_animism religion = bon_religion } # (les) ancêtres (Ritualistic/Bon get_the_ancestors)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_dela
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la moisson" (get_harvest_goddess_default)
		}
	}
}

			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Fortune (Roman get_fortuna)
				always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la fortune" (get_fortune_goddess_default)
			}
		}
	}
}

# Male Gods (Medicine) / Dieux de la médecine

	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_que
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Vetis (Etruscan get_vetis)
				religion = druidism # Belenos (Chaldean get_belenos)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Nusku (Chaldean get_nusku)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_qu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Esculape (Roman get_aesculapius)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Asclépios (Hellenic get_asclepius)
				religion = carthaginian_pantheon # Eshmoun (Canaanite get_eshmun)
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Imhotep (Kemetic get_imhotep)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_quele
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "dieu de la médecine" (get_medicine_god_default)
		}
	}

				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Tinia (Etruscan get_tinia)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Zeus (Hellenic get_zeus)
				religion = anatolian_religion # Sabazios (Cybelene get_sabazios)
				AND = { country_culture = carthaginian religion = carthaginian_pantheon } # Ba'l Hammon (Carthaginian get_baal_hammon)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = carthaginian } religion = carthaginian_pantheon } # Ba'l Shamin (Canaanite get_baalshamin)
				religion = druidism # Taranis (Druidic get_taranis)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_qu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Horus (Kemetic get_horus)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = assyrian } religion = mesopotamian_religion } # Enlil (Chaldean get_enlil)
				AND = { country_culture = assyrian religion = mesopotamian_religion } # Ashshur (Chaldean get_ashshur)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_quele
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "dieu du ciel" (get_sky_god_default)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
		}
	}
}

				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Déméter (Hellenic get_demeter)

				religion = anatolian_religion # Cybèle (Cybelene get_cybele)
				AND = { country_culture = aquitani religion = druidism } # Mari (Aquitani get_mari)
				religion = armenian_religion # Huba (Khaldic get_huba)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Shâla (Chaldean get_shala)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = aquitani } religion = druidism } # Rosmerta (Druidic get_rosmerta)
				religion = germanic_religion # Nerthuz (Tuistic get_nerthus)
				religion = matrist_religion # Saulia (Matrist get_saulia)
				religion = shamanism # Sémélé (Zalmoxian get_semele)
				religion = zoroaster # Spenta Armaiti (Zoroaster get_tishtrya)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Jewish get_jewish_god)
				religion = hindu # Parvati (Hindu get_parvati)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = jainism # Mahavira (Jain get_mahavir)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_qu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = egyptian_pantheon # Isis (Kemetic get_isis)
				religion = caucasian_religion # Anahit (Armazic get_anahit)
				religion = berber_religion # Isis (Megalithic get_isis)
				religion = indo_iranian_religion # Argimpasa (Heptadic get_argimpasa)
				religion = arabian_pantheon # ar-Rabba (Arabic get_orotalt)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_queles
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = animism # (les) Duillae (Iberic get_the_duillae)
				OR = { religion = eastern_animism religion = bon_religion } # (les) ancêtres (Ritualistic/Bon get_the_ancestors)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_quela
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la moisson" (get_harvest_goddess_default)
		}
	}
}
# Female Goddesses (Hearth) / Déesses du foyer
get_QueQueleQuela_hearth_goddess_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_que
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Vesta (Roman get_vesta)
				religion = mesopotamian_religion # Tashmêtu (Chaldean get_tashmetum)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_qu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Hestia (Hellenic get_hestia)
				religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_quela
		trigger = {
			always = yes # Fallback "déesse du foyer" (get_hearth_goddess_default)
		}
	}
}
# Female Goddesses (Fortune) / Déesses de la fortune
get_QueQueleQuela_fortune_goddess_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_que
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { country_culture = etruscan religion = roman_pantheon } # Nurtia (Etruscan get_nortia)
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture_group = latin } religion = roman_pantheon } # Tyché (Hellenic get_tyche)
				religion = buddhism # Bouddha (Buddhist get_buddha)
				religion = judaism # Yahvé (Yahvé get_jewish_god)
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_qu
		trigger = {
			religion = zoroaster # Ahura Mazda (Zoroaster get_zoroastrian_god)
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_quela
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = { NOT = { country_culture = etruscan } country_culture_group = latin religion = roman_pantheon } # Fortune (Roman get_fortuna)
				always = yes # Fallback "déesse de la fortune" (get_fortune_goddess_default)
			}
		}
	}
}



#########################################
# GOVERNMENT NAMES / RÉGIMES POLITIQUES #
#########################################
###Ex.: un[Ø]] royaume tribal / un[e] chefferie tribale
get_XEGouv_FR = {
	type = country
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_nothing
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				government = imperium # Empire
				government = imperial_cult # Culte impérial
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = frloc_e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				government = aristocratic_republic # République aristocratique
				government = theocratic_republic # République théocratique
				government = oligarchic_republic # République oligarchique
				government = democratic_republic # République démocratique
				government = plutocratic_republic # République ploutocratique
				government = dictatorship # Dictature
				government = despotic_monarchy # Monarchie autocratique
				government = aristocratic_monarchy # Monarchie aristocratique
				government = stratocratic_monarchy # Monarchie stratocratique
				government = theocratic_monarchy # Monarchie théocratique
				government = plutocratic_monarchy # Monarchie ploutocratique
				government = tribal_chiefdom # Tribu nomade
				government = tribal_kingdom # Tribu sédentarisée
				government = tribal_federation # Fédération tribale
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

				tradegood_pl_masc_vow_06 = yes

		}

}

	}

		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}
